  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 展示声明式交互协议（如EMAS）在工业级Agentic AI中的实际价值，并探索一条无需全面改造即可将形式化方法引入现有实践的技术路径。

Method: 将UCP结账部分建模为声明式Langshaw协议，使用Peach编程模型实现智能体，并与Google实现的UCP智能体进行互操作性验证。

Result: 成功建模UCP结账流程并实现Peach智能体与Google UCP智能体之间的互操作，验证了方法的保真度和可行性。

Conclusion: 声明式协议规范具有明确的形式化优势，且通过互操作可实现增量式工业落地，为EMAS思想影响实践提供了务实途径。

Abstract: The last few years have witnessed major advances in the modeling and implementation of multiagent systems based on declarative interaction protocols. Our contribution, Strabo, establishes the relevance of these advances to ongoing industry efforts in Agentic AI. Specifically, we consider UCP, the Universal Commerce Protocol, a recent Google-led effort to standardize e-commerce interactions for AI agents. Our exercise is in two parts. One, we model the part of UCP dealing with checkouts as a declarative Langshaw protocol and implement agents using Peach, a programming model for Langshaw. This part of the exercise brings out the advantages of formal, declarative specifications. Two, we show that Peach agents can interoperate with UCP agents implemented by Google, thereby establishing the fidelity of our approach with respect to UCP. Such interoperation enables the incremental introduction of declarative protocols and agents into a conventional setting, indicating a pathway by which EMAS ideas could influence practice without demanding a wholesale update.

### [229] [AutoLab: Can Frontier Models Solve Long-Horizon Auto Research and Engineering Tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05080)
*Zhangchen Xu,Junda Chen,Yue Huang,Dongfu Jiang,Jiefeng Chen,Hang Hua,Zijian Wu,Zheyuan Liu,Zexue He,Lichi Li,Shizhe Diao,Jiaxin Pei,Jinsung Yoon,Hao Zhang,Mengdi Wang,Radha Poovendran,Misha Sra,Alex Pentland,Zichen Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoLab是一个面向超长周期闭环优化任务的基准测试，包含36个跨四个领域的真实任务，评估发现模型成功的关键在于持续迭代和实证反馈整合能力，而非单次尝试质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估单轮响应或短周期智能体轨迹，无法捕捉长时间跨度下持续迭代改进的挑战，因此需要构建能反映真实科研工程长周期迭代过程的评估基准。

Method: 设计了36个由专家策划的跨领域任务（系统优化、谜题挑战、模型开发、CUDA内核优化），每个任务从正确但刻意次优的基线开始，在严格的时间预算内评估17个前沿模型的持续改进能力。

Result: 成功的关键预测因素是模型在反复基准测试、编辑和整合经验反馈方面的持久性；claude-opus-4.6表现出最强的长周期优化能力，而大多数前沿模型（包括多个闭源模型）要么提前终止，要么在预算内进展甚微。

Conclusion: 时间感知和持续迭代对自主智能体至关重要，开源完整的基准、评估框架和任务工件可加速长周期智能体研究。

Abstract: Scientific and engineering progress is fundamentally a long-horizon iterative process: proposing changes, running experiments, measuring outcomes, and continuously refining artifacts. Yet existing benchmarks for frontier models primarily evaluate either single-turn responses or short-horizon agent trajectories, failing to capture the challenges of sustained iterative improvement over extended time horizons. To address this gap, we introduce AutoLab, a new benchmark for ultra long-horizon closed-loop optimization. AutoLab consists of 36 realistic, expert-curated tasks spanning four diverse domains: system optimization, puzzle & challenge, model development, and CUDA kernel optimization. Each task begins with a correct but deliberately suboptimal baseline and challenges agents to improve it within a strict wall-clock budget. Evaluating 17 state-of-the-art models reveals the dominant predictor of success is not the quality of an agent's initial attempt, but its persistence in repeatedly benchmarking, editing, and incorporating empirical feedback. While claude-opus-4.6 exhibits strong long-horizon optimization capabilities, most frontier models, including several proprietary ones, either terminate prematurely or exhaust their budgets with minimal progress. These results underscore the importance of time awareness and persistent iteration in autonomous agents. We open-source the full benchmark, evaluation harness, and task artifacts, to accelerate research toward truly capable long-horizon agents.

### [230] [Knowledge Index of Noah's Ark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05104)
*Sheng Jin,Minghao Liu,Yunze Xiao,Zeqi Zhou,Heli Qi,Yifan Yao,Meishu Song,Kaijing Ma,Xuan Zhang,Sicong Jiang,Yizhe Li,Ningshan Ma,Jie Wei,Ziniu Li,Minglai Yang,Bangya Liu,Yiming Liang,Xiao Fang,Qingcheng Zeng,Jiarui Liu,Rui Yang,Shen Yan,Wenhao Huang,Jiaheng Liu,Zihan Wang,Weihao Xuan,Ge Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: KINA是一个包含899个题目、覆盖261个细粒度学科的大语言模型知识基准。通过代理优化实现学科代表性（近似比1-1/e），并证明奖金锦标赛机制在发布-评审质量上随机占优于固定支付（阈值B > ΔC/Δp_min）。在42个模型评估中，最高分Gemini-3.1-Pro-Preview仅53.17%，远未饱和；工具增强带来最多5.17分提升；通过自助法排名稳定性统计显式报告有限预算下的方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM知识基准存在三个问题：基于规模的扩展设计未能操作化学科代表性；固定报酬的标注方式纵容了懒惰共识；有限测试预算下排名不稳定且未经审计。作者旨在提出一个更严谨、更具学科代表性且激励相容的基准。

Method: (1) 代表性建模为覆盖式目标，通过专家引导锚点的代理目标实现学科代表性，给出(1-1/e)的贪心近似保证（Proposition 1）；(2) 设计奖金锦标赛机制（bonus-on-bar tournament），证明其在发布-评审质量上弱一阶随机占优于固定支付，激励相容阈值为B > ΔC/Δp_min（Theorem 1）；(3) 构建899题、261个细粒度学科的KINA基准；(4) 使用自助法计算排名稳定性统计量。

Result: 评估13个实验室的42个模型：最高分Gemini-3.1-Pro-Preview为53.17%，Claude-Opus-4.6为49.92%，GPT-5.4为48.55%；排名呈分层结构（前沿层>48%，强模型层38-45%，低性能层略高于10%随机基线）；工具增强最高提升5.17分，不同模型增益差异显著。

Conclusion: 现有LLM在细粒度学科知识上远未饱和，排名呈现分层而非平滑全序；工具增强效果因模型而异；有限预算下的排名方差应被显式报告以避免过度解读相邻排名差异。

Abstract: Knowledge benchmarks for LLMs face three issues: scaling-driven designs that do not operationalize disciplinary representativeness; flat-payment annotation that permits lazy consensus; and unaudited ranking instability under bounded test budgets. We introduce KINA, an 899-item benchmark across 261 fine-grained disciplines, with two formal results. First, we cast representativeness as a coverage-style objective over expert-elicited anchors and operationalize disciplinary representativeness through a proxy, yielding a (1-1/e) greedy approximation (Proposition 1); the guarantee applies to the proxy, not to population representativeness. Second, we prove a bonus-on-bar tournament weakly FOSD-dominates flat payment in released-review quality, with incentive-compatibility threshold B > Delta C / Delta p_min (Theorem 1). Evaluating 42 models from 13 labs, the top model, Gemini-3.1-Pro-Preview, reaches 53.17%, followed by Claude-Opus-4.6 at 49.92% and GPT-5.4 at 48.55%, leaving substantial headroom below saturation. The full leaderboard shows a tiered structure rather than a smooth total order: a small frontier tier lies above 48%, a dense strong-model tier spans roughly 38-45%, and low-performing models remain only modestly above the 10% chance baseline. Tool augmentation adds up to 5.17 points across the five tool-use evaluations, with gains varying substantially across models. We report bootstrap ranking-stability statistics to make bounded-budget variance explicit and to discourage over-interpretation of adjacent ranks.

### [231] [Polymarket-v1 Database](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04217)
*Boka Qin,Rui Yang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Polymarket-v1数据库，包含12亿条链上交易记录，并利用100%真实的交易方向数据评估了经典微观结构工具的性能，发现传统分类方法在预测市场中表现接近随机，且分类误差会向下游指标传播，最终影响预测市场设计推断的可靠性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预测市场数据存档依赖启发式推断交易方向，缺乏基于区块链结算层的真实交易方向数据，导致微观结构分析工具的有效性无法被准确评估。

Method: 构建了Polymarket-v1数据库，包含从第一笔结算到合约自然终止的全生命周期链上交易数据（2022-2026年），利用区块链结算层提供的100%真实交易方向，对tick规则、大额成交量分类等经典微观结构工具进行基准测试。

Conclusion: 交易层面的测量准确性是可靠推断预测市场设计和概率校准的前提，分类代理指标无法替代真实微观结构指标在预测市场分析中的作用。

Abstract: We introduce the Polymarket-v1 Database: the complete on-chain trade archive of Polymarket's first-generation CTF Exchange on Polygon, spanning 2022-11-21 to 2026-04-28 and covering the full contract lifecycle from first settlement to natural termination. The dataset comprises 1.20 billion trade records across 1.30 million markets with $61 billion in nominal volume. Its defining feature is 100% ground-truth aggressor direction derived from the blockchain settlement layer, a property unavailable in existing prediction market archives, which rely on heuristic inference. We use this truth-aligned archive to benchmark standard microstructure tools and document three findings. First, the tick rule and bulk volume classification achieve near-random aggregate accuracy (49.83% and 50.51%), but this masks a systematic, correctable price-level gradient driven by positive trade direction autocorrelation and concentrated market-making -- two structural features of prediction markets that violate the mean-reversion assumption embedded in classical classifiers. Second, these classification errors propagate into downstream metrics: inferred VPIN diverges substantially from ground-truth VPIN, and OFI estimates are directionally biased, with material consequences for Transaction Cost Analysis. Third, ground-truth microstructure quality predicts forecasting performance in ways that classification-based proxies cannot recover: True VPIN positively predicts Brier scores, while Gibbs spread negatively predicts them -- a selection effect reflecting that high-spread niche markets attract informed specialists rather than noise traders. Replacing ground-truth metrics with classified proxies attenuates both relationships, illustrating that measurement accuracy at the transaction level is a prerequisite for reliable inference about prediction market design and probability calibration.

### [232] [Dead Science Walking: Publication Bias and the AI Scientist Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04220)
*Kargi Chauhan*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: AI科学家系统会因训练语料中阳性结果过多、阴性结果不足而产生"语料库失效"风险，导致对科学盲点的加速放大，本文量化了这一偏差并提出治理方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI科学家系统正自动化产生、评估和迭代科学假说，但其速度优势也会同步放大科学记录中固有的偏差（阳性结果过代表、阴性结果不足），这一近端风险尚未被充分关注和量化。

Method: 形式化定义了"零结果差距"（null result gap），在药物发现（~0.60）、心理学（~0.56）和癌症生物学（~0.35）三个领域进行估计；引入"放大指数"（amplification index）分析检索-生成-自动评估三阶段流水线如何复合放大原始偏差，给出2.18倍的放大因子估计。

Result: 标准三阶段流水线可将语料库偏差放大2.18倍，且该结论在更保守的乘数假设下依然成立。识别出四种治理失败模式：自信重发现、幽灵证据积累、复制洗白和置信度校准失调。

Conclusion: AI科学家不仅会加速科学发现，若无治理，它们会先加速科学盲点。提出三项干预措施：零结果数据库作为训练基础设施、撤销感知评估指标、强制性训练语料库披露。

Abstract: AI scientist systems are beginning to automate the production, evaluation, and iteration of scientific hypotheses. Their promise is speed; their risk is that speed also scales errors embedded in the scientific record. We argue that a near-term risk is corpus failure: AI scientist systems are trained on and grounded in a literature that over-represents positive results and under-represents null findings. We formalise this distortion as the null result gap, estimate it across three domains (drug discovery ~0.60, psychology ~0.56, cancer biology ~0.35), and introduce an amplification index for reasoning about how retrieval, generation, and automated evaluation can compound the raw gap. Using first-order estimates, we argue that a standard three-stage pipeline can amplify corpus distortion by a factor of 2.18x, with the conclusion unchanged under more conservative multipliers. We identify four governance failure modes: confident rediscovery, ghost evidence accumulation, replication laundering, and confidence miscalibration. We then propose three interventions: null-result databases as training infrastructure, retraction-aware evaluation metrics, and mandatory training corpus disclosure. The central takeaway is that AI scientists will not only accelerate science. Without governance, they will accelerate science's blind spots before they accelerate its discoveries.

</details>


### [233] [When Does Structure Help? The Information Bonus of AlphaFold2 Representations over Protein Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04228)
*Kargi Chauhan*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出信息奖励(IB)指标，量化冷冻单序列AlphaFold2 Evoformer表示与ESM-2嵌入在蛋白质任务中的性能差异。实验表明：ESM-2在结合亲和力回归和构象灵活性分类上占优，AF2仅在别构位点分类上提供优势。同时发现残基级数据泄露会严重干扰模型排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AI科学家系统中，选择生物学基础模型先于实验选择成为趋势。蛋白质管线面临具体工程与科学问题：结构推理的成本何时值得高于更便宜的序列模型？需要一个可量化的指标来指导表示选择决策。

Method: 提出信息奖励(IB)指标，在蛋白质级交叉验证下测量冷冻单序列AlphaFold2 Evoformer表示与ESM-2嵌入的线性可及优势。在结合亲和力回归(PDBbind, n=5,680)、构象灵活性(ATLAS分子动力学, 268个蛋白质)和别构位点分类(AlloSigDB, n=9,925残基)三个任务上评估。

Result: ESM-2主导结合亲和力(IB=-0.141; Pearson r=0.449 vs. 0.307)和二值灵活性分类(IB=-0.060; AUROC 0.824 vs. 0.764; p=0.0017)。AF2单表示在别构预测上唯一优于随机水平(IB=+0.064; AUROC 0.548 vs. 0.485)。发现残基级数据泄露使RMSF性能虚高27-39%，足以逆转表示排名。

Conclusion: IB指标将表示选择转化为可衡量的决策。序列模型在大多数情况下足够且更优，结构信息仅在需要长程几何信号的别构预测中提供额外价值。研究强调了数据泄露评估在模型比较中的重要性。

Abstract: AI scientist systems increasingly choose biological foundation models before they choose experiments. In protein pipelines, this creates a concrete engineering and scientific question: when is the cost of structural inference worth paying over a cheaper sequence-only model? We introduce the information bonus (IB), a task-level metric that measures the linearly accessible advantage of frozen single-sequence AlphaFold2 Evoformer representations over frozen ESM-2 embeddings under protein-level cross-validation. Across binding affinity regression (PDBbind, n=5,680), conformational flexibility (ATLAS molecular dynamics, 268 proteins), and allosteric-site classification (AlloSigDB, n=9,925 residues), IB is sharply mechanism-dependent. ESM-2 dominates binding affinity (IB=-0.141; Pearson r=0.449 vs. 0.307) and binary flexibility (IB=-0.060; AUROC 0.824 vs. 0.764; p=0.0017). AF2 single representations give the only above-chance allostery predictions (IB=+0.064; AUROC 0.548 vs. 0.485), revealing long-range geometric signal not recovered from sequence alone. We also identify a residue-level leakage artifact: naive residue splits inflate RMSF performance by 27-39% depending on the representation, enough to reverse representation rankings. These results turn representation selection into a measurable decision for AI-for-science systems.

### [234] [Learning to cooperate with emergent reputation via multi-agent reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04359)
*Xinwei Song,Yizhe Huang,Dengji Zhao,Xue Feng*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出COOPER方法，一种分布式多智能体强化学习框架，能够完全从环境奖励中联合学习声誉评估规则和基于声誉的策略，解决了传统方法依赖预定义声誉规则或内在奖励的问题，在捐赠博弈和硬币博弈实验中展现出良好的泛化性和适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么使用预定义的声誉评估规则，要么将声誉建模为内在奖励来学习策略，这损害了方法的泛化和适应能力。因此，需要一种能够完全从环境奖励中联合学习声誉评估规则和基于声誉的策略的方法。

Method: 提出COOPER（COOPeration with Emergent Reputation），一种分布式多智能体强化学习方法，利用声誉的内在机制精心设计各组成模块及其数据流，克服了声誉与策略深度纠缠导致的反馈信号延迟和噪声问题，实现从环境奖励中联合学习声誉评估规则和基于声誉的策略。

Abstract: Reputation, the aggregation of peer assessments diffused through social networks, is a pivotal mechanism for promoting cooperation in social dilemmas ubiquitous to distributed multi-agent systems comprising agents with limited perception and cognitive capabilities. Exploring efficient reputation systems, comprising reputation assessment rules and reputation-based policies, is a long-standing challenge. Previous work assumes predefined reputation assessment rules or models reputation as an intrinsic reward to learn policies, compromising the methods' ability for generalization and adaptation. To address this, we propose a distributed multi-agent reinforcement learning method $\textbf{COOPER}$ ($\textbf{COOP}$eration with $\textbf{E}$mergent $\textbf{R}$eputation), which jointly learns reputation assessment rules and reputation-based policies entirely from environment rewards. Notably, leveraging the underlying mechanisms of reputation, we deliberately design the constituent modules of $\textbf{COOPER}$ and the data flows among them, overcoming the latency and noise in the feedback signal, caused by the deep entanglement between reputation and policy. Experiments on the donation game and the coin game in grid world environments demonstrate that $\textbf{COOPER}$ effectively adapts to various existing reputation systems and co-players. Furthermore, we observe the co-emergence of reputation norms and cooperation in self-play settings. These results hold robustly across diverse social network topologies, underscoring the generalizability and efficacy of our approach.

</details>


### [235] [Improved Approximation Guarantees for Groupwise Maximin Share Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04731)
*Georgios Amanatidis,Anna Korfiati,Evangelos Markakis,Christodoulos Santorinaios*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究不可分割商品公平分配中的群组最大最小份额公平性（GMMS），提出了一个多项式时间算法，将近似比从之前的4/7提升至(φ-1)≈0.618，并在三代理情形下进一步改进至约0.72。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GMMS公平分配算法的近似比仅为4/7，存在改进空间；同时需要更深入地理解在多代理子集约束下最大化份额的计算与逼近难题。

Method: 提出一种保持Draft-and-Eliminate算法主要性质的简化算法，通过仔细分析任意代理子集所诱导子实例中相关价值的界来改进近似比；针对三代理情形，通过部分刻画短挑选序列的最大最小份额保证来进一步提升。

Result: 实现了(φ-1)≈0.618的全局近似比（渐近最优），并将三代理情形的近似比改进至(√10-1)/3≈0.72。

Conclusion: 所提算法在保持已有算法良好性质的同时显著提升了GMMS近似保证，其分析在同类算法中渐近最优，并为受限设定（如代理对top n商品一致或代理数较少时）提供了更好的保障。

Abstract: We study the problem of fairly allocating a set of indivisible goods to a set of $n$ agents with additive valuation functions. We focus on the very demanding notion of \textit{groupwise maximin share fairness} (GMMS), which requires that each agent $i$ receives value comparable to their maximin share, where the latter is computed \textit{with respect to any subset of agents that contains $i$}. We show that it is possible to compute $(φ-1)$-approximate GMMS allocations in polynomial time, where $φ\approx 1.618$ is the golden ratio). This improves on the previously known guarantee of $4/7$ of Chaudhury et al. [SICOMP; 2021] and Amanatidis et al. [TCS; 2020]. We propose a simple algorithm that maintains the same main properties as the Draft-and-Eliminate algorithm of Amanatidis et al. [TCS, 2020] and we improve on the approximation guarantee analysis by carefully bounding the relevant value within any subinstance induced by the restriction of our allocation to a subset of agents. Our analysis is asymptotically tight for algorithms that share these properties and has the additional benefit of giving improved guarantees for restricted settings; in particular, when the agents agree on the top $n$ goods or when the number of agents is small. To illustrate the challenges of going beyond the guarantees of our algorithm, we also present a variant with an improved approximation of $(\sqrt{10}-1)/3 \approx 0.72$ for the case of three agents. To achieve this improvement we partially characterize the maximin share guarantees of short picking sequences for a small number of goods.

</details>


### [236] [Extending the El Farol Bar Game with Partial Observability and Incentive Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04753)
*Iosif Polenakis,Kalliopi Kastampolidou,Theodore Andronikos*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文将经典的El Farol Bar博弈重构为酒吧(作为具备AI学习能力的机制设计者)与有限理性 agents(采用AI学习策略)之间的双边学习系统，通过动态定价与部分可观测性，探索协调演化的新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统El Farol Bar问题中酒吧仅作为被动容量约束存在，忽略了场所本身可以通过策略性干预(如动态定价)影响协调结果的可能性。作者旨在将酒吧从被动约束转变为主动机制设计者，以更真实地刻画复杂自适应系统中的协调问题。

Method: (1) 引入部分可观测性：agents仅能观察到历史参与者的子集；(2) 将酒吧建模为具备AI学习能力的策略性玩家，通过策略学习优化动态定价，平衡收入、利用率和可持续性；(3) agents使用AI学习形成信念并调整参与策略；(4) 构建双边学习系统，将协调问题建模为有限理性agents与自适应机构之间的协同演化过程。

Result: 提出了一个两方学习框架，其中agents和酒吧各自通过AI学习方法适应彼此的策略，形成了协同演化的动态过程。

Conclusion: 该框架为拥堵管理、资源分配和机制设计等复杂自适应系统问题提供了新的理论视角，揭示了机构设计者可以通过动态策略干预引导协调结果的机制。

Abstract: The El Farol Bar game is a classic model of coordination under uncertainty, traditionally treating the venue as a passive constraint. In this work, we re-conceptualize the problem by modeling the bar as a strategic player equipped with AI-driven learning capabilities. We extend the original framework to include partial observability, i.e., agents observe only subsets of past attendees, and transform the bar from a passive capacity threshold into an active mechanism designer that adjusts pricing policies to balance revenue, utilization, and sustainability constraints. Agents employ AI-based learning to form beliefs and adapt attendance strategies under incomplete information, while the bar uses policy learning to optimize dynamic pricing. The resulting two-sided learning system frames coordination as a co-evolutionary process between boundedly rational agents and an adaptive institution, offering insights into congestion management, resource allocation, and mechanism design in complex adaptive systems.

</details>


### [237] [Welfare Maximization in Bilateral Trade: Improved Approximation Guarantees Beyond the Fixed Price Barrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04890)
*Shahar Dobzinski,Ariel Shaulker*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究双边贸易中的社会福利最大化问题，证明了带有保留价的买方报价机制能达到0.746的社会福利近似比，超越了固定价格机制0.72的上限，并首次证明固定价格机制在该问题中并非最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已几乎精确刻画了固定价格机制在双边贸易社会福利最大化中的近似比（约0.72-0.7381），但尚无其他激励相容机制能超越固定价格机制的性能，因此需要探索其他机制类别以取得更好的社会福利保证。

Method: 研究买方报价机制（buyer-offering mechanism with a reserve price）。在该机制中，买方根据自身价值做出"接受或放弃"的报价，且报价不低于预设的保留价；卖方的最优策略是当自己的成本不高于报价时接受。通过理论分析证明存在一个保留价能保证0.746的社会福利近似比。

Result: 证明了存在一个保留价使得买方报价机制能获得至少0.746倍的最优社会福利，超越了固定价格机制已知的最好近似比（0.72），同时也突破了固定价格机制的上界（0.7381）。

Conclusion: 固定价格机制在双边贸易社会福利最大化中并非最优，买方报价机制能取得更好的近似比保证。

Abstract: We study the setting of welfare maximization in bilateral trade, where the values of both the buyer and the seller are drawn from independent distributions. Our goal is to maximize social welfare. In this setting, fixed price mechanisms have been extensively studied. In a fixed price mechanism, there is a price $p$ that depends only on the distributions of the buyer and the seller. Trade occurs if and only if the buyer's value is at least $p$ and the seller's value is at most $p$. A long line of work has culminated in determining almost exactly the approximation ratios achievable by fixed price mechanisms: there exists a fixed price mechanism that obtains at least a $0.72$ fraction of the social welfare, but no fixed price mechanism can guarantee more than a $0.7381$ fraction of it [Cai and Wu, STOC'23; Liu, Ren, and Wang, STOC'23]. No other incentive-compatible mechanism is known to beat the performance of fixed-price mechanisms in this setting.
  This paper shows how to achieve a larger fraction of the optimal welfare with other classes of mechanisms. Specifically, we study the buyer-offering mechanism with a reserve price. In this mechanism, the buyer observes its value and makes a take-it-or-leave-it offer to the seller, where the offer is at least the reserve price. Beyond its simplicity, this natural mechanism is attractive because the seller always has a dominant strategy: accept the offer if its value is at most the offer, and otherwise reject it. We show that there always exists a reserve price that guarantees a $0.746$ fraction of the social welfare. This not only improves upon the best previously known approximation guarantee for the problem, but also demonstrates that fixed-price mechanisms are not optimal in this setting.

</details>


### [238] [Fairness and Strategy-Proofness in Automated Market Makers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04959)
*Frank M. V. Feys*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文证明在包含三个及以上资产的加权乘积自动做市商中，不存在同时满足公平性和防策略性的流动性提供者投票聚合规则。公平性要求均值型聚合，防策略性要求中位数型聚合，唯一同时满足两者的规则是单一提供者独裁。这一障碍在只有两个资产时消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动做市商（AMM）不允许流动性提供者对交易函数进行投票，本文旨在探究这一现象背后的结构性原因，而非偶然疏忽。

Method: 采用社会选择理论的阿罗式框架，分析加权乘积家族AMM中流动性提供者偏好聚合的公平性与防策略性条件，并利用Frongillo-Papireddygari-Waggoner等价性将结果与外部贝叶斯池化问题联系起来。

Result: 在n≥3个资产时，公平性迫使采用加权Aitchison质心（加权几何平均）形式的聚合规则，但这是均值型聚合；而防策略性要求中位数型聚合。唯一同时满足两种性质的规则是独裁。当n=2时，存在公平且防策略的规则。

Conclusion: AMM中不允许流动性提供者对交易函数投票是结构性必然，而非设计疏忽。该不可能性结果与外部贝叶斯池化的不可能性等价，揭示了AMM设计中基本的权衡限制。

Abstract: No deployed automated market maker lets its liquidity providers vote on the trading function. We show this is structural, not an oversight. On the weighted-product family with $n \geq 3$ assets, no aggregation rule is at once fair and strategy-proof. Arrovian fairness forces a unique form, the weighted Aitchison centroid, the weighted geometric mean of the providers' preferred pools. But fairness forces mean-type aggregation and strategy-proofness forces median-type, and the only rule that is both is a single-provider dictator. The obstruction is sharp: it vanishes at $n = 2$, where a fair strategy-proof rule exists. Under the Frongillo--Papireddygari--Waggoner equivalence, the centroid is Genest's logarithmic opinion pool, and the impossibility transfers to externally Bayesian pooling.

</details>


### [239] [Non-obvious Manipulability in the Additively Separable Group Activity Selection Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05048)
*Maria Fomenko,Giovanna Varricchio*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究非完全信息下可加可分离群组活动选择问题(AS-GASP)的机制设计，目标是同时实现社会福利最大化和防止策略性操纵（非明显可操纵性，NOM）。主要结论包括：当偏好和权重为任意或非负时，最优机制满足NOM；但当偏好或权重为二值时，最优性与NOM可能不兼容。计算方面，任意值下无有界近似比算法，非负偏好下则存在渐近最优且满足NOM的近似机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在群组活动选择中，代理人对活动有私人偏好，同时对其他代理人有私人权重（即希望/不希望与谁同组）。传统研究大多假设完全信息，本文致力于在不完全信息（私人信息）环境下设计防操纵的机制，以最大化社会福利。

Method: 采用非明显可操纵性(NOM)作为防操纵的松弛概念；通过理论分析研究最优机制与NOM的兼容性（在不同偏好/权重取值域下）；建立计算复杂性和不可近似性结果；设计满足NOM的近似机制。

Result: 1) 任意或非负偏好/权重下，最优机制满足NOM；二值情形下最优性与NOM不兼容。2) 任意值下AS-GASP无有界近似比多项式算法。3) 非负偏好下存在渐近最优且满足NOM的近似机制。

Conclusion: AS-GASP在非完全信息下，机制的可操纵性与最优性之间存在复杂权衡，但在非负偏好等实际常见设定中，可以同时实现近似最优和防操纵。

Abstract: In this work, we study the additively separable Group Activity Selection Problem (AS-GASP) in an imperfect information setting, where agents have private preferences over activities and weights over other agents. Our goal is to design mechanisms that assign agents to activities based on their declared preferences and weights, with the objective of maximizing social welfare while ensuring truthful reporting. We, therefore, focus on the notion of non-obvious manipulability (NOM), a form of resilience to manipulation. We first investigate the relationship between NOM and social welfare optimality. In this regard, our main result shows that, when preferences and weights are arbitrary or non-negative, any optimal mechanism is non-obviously manipulable. In contrast, when either preferences or weights are binary, we show that optimality and NOM may be incompatible. We then turn to computational aspects. While it is known that computing an optimal outcome for the AS-GASP is NP-hard even in restricted settings, we establish a strong inapproximability result showing that no polynomial-time algorithm can guarantee a bounded approximation ratio when preferences and weights may take arbitrary values. In turn, when preferences are non-negative, we show that a bounded approximation is possible, and we present two asymptotically optimal approximation mechanisms that are also guaranteed to satisfy NOM.

</details>


### [240] [Gradient Dynamics in First-Price Auctions: Iterative Strategy Elimination via Cubic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05108)
*Mete Şeref Ahunbay,Weiqiang Zheng,Tao Lin*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 在离散化一级价格完全信息拍卖中，采用在线梯度上升学习的买方在时间平均意义上几乎能实现二级价格拍卖的高效结果。该证明基于两个创新：基于势函数的博弈论分析框架（可迭代消除特定策略），以及一类三次"候选势函数"（确保在线梯度上升在概率单纯形上对二次策略修改无遗憾）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在线学习算法（在线梯度上升）在离散化一级价格拍卖中的均衡收敛性质，探究学习动态能否导向高效的市场结果。

Method: 1. 提出基于势函数的论证方法，分析正规形式博弈中梯度上升的时间平均策略行为，提供可迭代应用的充分条件，类似迭代消除劣势策略。2. 构造一类三次候选势函数，分类概率单纯形上的一族二次策略修改，证明在线梯度上升对这些修改无遗憾。

Result: 在离散化一级价格完全信息拍卖中，买方采用在线梯度上升学习时，时间平均结果接近于二级价格拍卖的高效结果。

Conclusion: 在线学习动态（梯度上升）可以引导一级价格拍卖走向近似高效的市场配置，为拍卖设计中的学习动态分析提供了新工具。

Abstract: We show that in discretised first-price auctions with complete information, if the buyers learn to bid with online gradient ascent, in time-average the outcome is (almost) the efficient outcome of the second-price auction. Our proof rests on two novel innovations in the analysis of online gradient ascent in normal-form games, which may be useful in a wider range of applications. First, we develop a potential-function-based argument for the analysis of gradient ascent in normal-form games, allowing us to deduce that certain strategies will not be played in time-average. We provide sufficient conditions which ensure this argument can be applied iteratively, resulting in a procedure reminiscent of iterative elimination of dominated strategies. Second, we develop a novel class of cubic "candidate potential functions", classifying a family of quadratic strategy modifications on the probability simplex against which online gradient ascent incurs no regret.

</details>
